### 1. iPhone 街头自然抓拍提示词

**Author**: [babydoll](https://x.com/bananababydoll)  **Date**: 2026-03-30  **Language**: en

> 这是一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，旨在模拟在城市人行道上，于清晨柔和阳光下拍摄的真实感智能手机照片，侧重于自然风格、淡妆效果以及逼真的动态模糊感。

![iPhone 街头自然抓拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774939624933_n7l5im_HDnVAqqWEAAEczi.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "camera": "iPhone 17 Pro",
    "lens": "35mm",
    "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
    "style": "natural iphone daylight, soft HDR, no heavy contrast, realistic skin texture"
  },
  "scene": {
    "location": "city sidewalk outside {argument name="location type" default="coffee shop"}",
    "time": "9:12 AM",
    "atmosphere": "quiet morning, soft sun, casual street life"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "primary": "natural soft morning sunlight",
    "effect": "gentle highlights on hair, even skin tones"
  },
  "subject": {
    "appearance": "tall blonde american model, minimal makeup, effortless beauty",
    "pose": {
      "position": "walking out holding iced coffee",
      "body": "natural stride, shoulders relaxed",
      "head": "slightly turned mid-step"
    },
    "expression": {
      "eyes": "half-focused, casual",
      "mouth": "soft neutral",
      "energy": "unbothered, naturally attractive"
    },
    "hair": {
      "style": "loose blonde hair, slightly messy morning texture"
    },
    "outfit": {
      "top": {
        "type": "fitted ribbed tank",
        "color": "muted olive"
      },
      "bottom": {
        "type": "low-rise relaxed jeans",
        "color": "washed blue"
      }
    }
  },
  "camera": {
    "angle": "slightly off-center candid",
    "distance": "mid shot",
    "imperfection": "tiny motion blur from walking"
  }
}
```

### 3. Y2K 梦幻特写肖像，支持面部特征锁定

**Author**: [Puneet Kharbanda](https://x.com/KPuneet20)  **Date**: 2026-03-30  **Language**: en

> 这是一份专为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示词，旨在生成具有特定服装、妆容和 90 年代颗粒感美学的梦幻 Y2K 风格特写肖像。该提示词明确要求使用参考图像，以确保 100% 还原面部特征。

![Y2K 梦幻特写肖像，支持面部特征锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774939633174_u1afaj_HEnrD4bbIAAkmfp.jpg)

```
Create a dreamy, close-up portrait in {argument name="style" default="Y2K"} style, with voluminous hair styled in loose waves. I pose with my back slightly turned to the camera, looking over my shoulder with a confident and sensual expression. My makeup is natural yet glamorous, with defined eyebrows, voluminous lashes, and glossy brown lips outlined with a brown lip liner. I'm wearing a tight-fitting, long-sleeved white dress with a black watercolor print, an off-the-shoulder neckline, and an open back, with slight ruching at the lower back to accentuate my curves. The fabric fits my figure perfectly. My skin is flawless and glowing under the camera flash, which illuminates my skin and dress. I accessorize with a long gold necklace that drapes down my back, several gold bracelets and rings, a diamond engagement ring, and a small black leather shoulder bag by Coco Chanel. The photo should have a grainy 90s aesthetic, with a textured stone wall in neutral tones behind me, and the flash creating a dark and slightly shadowed background. Maintain 100% exact facial features as the reference image; Facial identity lock — use the provided reference face; preserve 100% of facial features (eyes, brows, nose, lips, jawline, proportions, skin tone and texture, expression, hairstyle). No beautification, replacement, or changes to the face.
```

```
The subject is standing and leaning back against an ornate grand piano, with both arms spread and resting along the piano edge. Her head is slightly tilted back, with a relaxed, sultry pose and parted lips.

She is wearing a black satin corset top with a low sweetheart neckline and front hook-and-eye closures, paired with black leather pants.

Lighting is direct front flash, creating high contrast with strong shadows cast onto the back wall.
```

```
Technical architectural blueprint of a Classic Smash Burger on deep navy drafting paper. Hyperrealistic food hero centered-left, dramatically lit from upper left, warm studio spotlight, cross-section view revealing every layer in precise stack order, lacy-edged patties visible in full photorealistic color, cheese mid-cascade, bun toasted golden, sauce pooling at base catching warm light. Labels connected by thin glowing CAD elbow-joint lines, no crossovers: "{argument name="label 1" default="BRIOCHE BUN sesame-crowned, butter-toasted, 11cm diameter"}" "{argument name="label 2" default="SMASH PATTY ×2  80/20 chuck, 85g each, crust-temp 220°C"}"  "{argument name="label 3" default="AMERICAN CHEESE  single-fold melt, 2 slices, full cascade}"  "CARAMELIZED ONION  45min low-heat, moisture-reduced, dark"  "BREAD & BUTTER PICKLE  4mm slice, brine-bright, translucent"  "HOUSE SAUCE  thousand island base, 18g applied, amber". Labels clustered right and top, white Helvetica Neue Light uppercase, thin italic descriptors below. Compass rose bottom-left, scale bar bottom-center, revision block top-right. Title block double-border bottom-right: "DISH: THE SMASH // CLASSIFICATION: AMERICAN CLASSIC // BUILD SPEC: Engineered to be the last burger you ever need." 4K, tack sharp, electric blue linework glowing softly, warm golden burger tones popping against cool navy. Style ref: Blade Runner 2049 meets hyperreal CGI food campaign. 4K, ultra sharp, chromatic aberration on edges, craveable.
```

### 14. 豪华顶层公寓夜景写实人像

### 23. 三联画混合媒介时尚构图

**Author**: [Cherry 2.O](https://x.com/Mind_Boticni)  **Date**: 2026-03-29  **Language**: en

> 这是为 Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro 编写的提示词，旨在创作一张高分辨率、照片级逼真的三联画构图，将女性形象融入抽象的混合媒介拼贴背景中，并详细描述了每个画面的姿势、服装和艺术风格。

![三联画混合媒介时尚构图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853740749_9cm7ak_HEkTrglbQAEdw-d.jpg)

```
A high-resolution, photorealistic three-panel composition featuring a woman with long, voluminous wavy brown hair and elegant features, integrated into an abstract mixed-media collage background.
Panel Layout:

Left Panel (Vertical, full height):

A tall portrait of the woman looking upwards at a dramatic angle, wearing a mustard yellow turtleneck. Cinematic lighting highlights her face and hair, with strong shadows and depth.
Top Right Panel (Square):

A close-up angled side profile, soft gaze to the right, wearing a black modern blazer with minimal jewelry. Expression is calm and confident.
Bottom Right Panel (Square):

A slightly top-down perspective, playful yet elegant pose, wearing a white textured dress, subtle smile, natural lighting.
Art Style & Background (applies to all panels):

The image is layered with an abstract mixed-media collage background incorporating geometric shapes like circles and rectangles in ochre, burnt orange, and charcoal grey. Include textural elements such as vintage parchment paper, blueprint-style technical sketches, and subtle floral etchings. Use a flat graphic design overlay that partially blends into each outfit, seamlessly merging the 3D subject with 2D modernist art.
Overall Style:

Cinematic lighting, fine art photography aesthetic, ultra-detailed, 8K resolution, modern editorial fashion magazine layout.
```

### 24. Starbucks Frappuccino 高端摄影棚广告视觉设计

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2026-03-29  **Language**: en

> 这是一份针对 Nano Banana Pro 的详细提示词，旨在引导其担任资深艺术总监，为 Starbucks Frappuccino 创作一张照片级逼真的 CGI 摄影棚广告视觉图。提示词涵盖了画布尺寸、背景颜色、水印图案、Logo 位置、产品摆放、光照条件及技术规格，旨在营造高端奢侈品牌的视觉美感。

![Starbucks Frappuccino 高端摄影棚广告视觉设计](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853727351_g1j67x_HEkS76YaYAE_lOB.jpg)
![Starbucks Frappuccino 高端摄影棚广告视觉设计](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853727384_fzkh5l_HEkS7_dbkAAKkGi.jpg)
![Starbucks Frappuccino 高端摄影棚广告视觉设计](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853727370_qhx200_HEkS7_bacAAZlGX.jpg)
![Starbucks Frappuccino 高端摄影棚广告视觉设计](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853728114_okb20f_HEkS8HmbMAASRzx.jpg)

```
Act as a senior art director and studio photographer for high-end advertising campaigns and e-commerce.

Format & Canvas
Vertical 9 :16. Background: {argument name="background color" default="warm off-white (# F4EFE6)"} or a neutral tone characteristic of the brand, with no visible shadows.

Background Pattern
Apply the brand’s signature motif as a large, tone-on-tone watermark (10–18% opacity). Motif size should be 15–25% of the canvas width, with a soft, slightly embossed feel.

Logo Placement
Position the Starbucks logo centered in the upper third. Width: 40–50% of the canvas. Use a flat, two-dimensional rendering in official brand colors.
Place the wordmark below the logo in spaced uppercase letters, matching the logo color. Wordmark height: approximately 60% of the logo height.

Product Placement
Photorealistic Starbucks frappuccino with full material fidelity (cup, lid, straw, textures, branding details).
Position: bottom right, angled at 25–35°. Cropped at 60–75%, occupying 55–65% of the canvas.
Use soft contact shadows (8–12% opacity), with no harsh shadows.

Lighting
Soft, directional daylight (5500–6000K). Key light from top left, fill from the right.
Minimal contrast (1.2–1.5:1), with global illumination for subtle light bounce.
No edge highlights; reflections only on metallic elements. Avoid hard shadows.

Typography & Finishing
At the bottom: a thin horizontal line (1 px, 80% width, in brand color).
Below it: microcopy ({argument name="microcopy text" default="social link or collection tag"}) in a clean sans-serif font, aligned with the context.

Technical Specifications
Photorealistic CGI (KeyShot/Octane style), 9: 16, ultra-high detail, f/16 depth of field, sharp edges, neutral color accuracy, slightly warm background, no environmental reflections.
Mood reference: official visuals from Louis Vuitton / Bottega Veneta / Celine.
```

[[Luxury Brand Aesthetic]] [[Product Placement]]

### 27. 身穿拼图毛衣的童趣角色 3D 渲染图

**Author**: [K](https://x.com/ChillaiKalan__)  **Date**: 2026-03-29  **Language**: en

> 这是一条专为 Google Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示词，旨在生成一张高细节、干净的 3D 渲染图。角色需具备柔和的童趣特征（无成人特征、无胡须、脸颊更饱满），身穿拼图图案毛衣，强调柔和的电影级光效以及丰富的蓝色渐变背景。

![身穿拼图毛衣的童趣角色 3D 渲染图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853742219_k8jl77_HEjWkEDbkAAZOXA.jpg)

```
soft, round face
fuller cheeks
small chin
slightly larger, expressive eyes (but still identity-consistent)
no beard, no sharp jawline, no adult features
Expression should be innocent, warm, and slightly playful, with a gentle smile and direct eye contact.
Body proportions should be cute and childlike (small, slightly chubby body, slightly larger head).

Pose: relaxed standing with hands behind the back, with a subtle natural tilt in head and shoulders to avoid stiffness.
Hair should match the reference but appear soft, slightly voluminous, and naturally styled, not overly sharp or artificial.
Skin should be soft and stylized, with subtle subsurface scattering (SSS) for a warm glow, matte finish (no plastic shine), and gentle natural blush on cheeks.
The character wears a half sleeves cotton sweater with a puzzle pattern, where:

colors are soft but lively and slightly vibrant
not oversaturated and not washed out
The fabric shows a realistic knit texture and soft folds
Lighting should be soft and cinematic:

key light from upper-left
gentle fill light
subtle rim light on hair
Background should be a rich blue gradient, brighter behind the subject and darker toward the edges, with smooth depth (not flat).
Output should be:

1:1 aspect ratio
mid-length framing (head to waist)
high-detail, clean 3D render
film-quality finish (not toy-like, not overly realistic)
```

[[Blue Gradient Background]]

> 这是用于 Nano Banana 2 的提示词，旨在生成一张 Millie Bobby Brown 在霓虹闪烁的游戏厅中的写实风格现代生活照，展现 E-Girl/软朋克美学，并手持 Kuromi 毛绒玩具摆出俏皮姿势。

![E-Girl 软朋克风游戏厅人像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853732984_j3xoz1_HEix8H4aoAAaCAW.jpg)
![E-Girl 软朋克风游戏厅人像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853732966_ga7egt_HEix8INXsAApyl3.jpg)
![E-Girl 软朋克风游戏厅人像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853733076_l3b2ly_HEix8F6W0AAr-h_.jpg)

```
"A fotorrealistic, modern lifestyle photo of {argument name="subject name" default="Millie Bobby Brown"}, smiling brightly and looking directly at the camera. She is crouching on a smooth concrete floor in a vibrant, neon-lit arcade, balancing on black chunky platform boots with straps and silver buckles. Her dark brown hair is styled in long pigtails with loose strands. She wears light makeup, a silver pendant necklace, a white bandeau top, a white mini-skirt with side slit and buckles, and spiked black leather wristbands. She holds a Kuromi plushie, featuring a black jester hat with a pink skull, in front of her chest. To her left is a large, brightly illuminated yellow claw machine filled with pastel plushies. The background features other colourful arcade games and glowing neon signs. The lighting is vibrant with strong yellow and magenta neon glow from the claw machine and diffuse ambient light. The scene has a playful, energetic, e-girl, soft punk vibe. ### 44. Nano Banana Pro 四格漫画提示词：时间停止喜剧
```

**Author**: [とりにく](https://x.com/tori29umai)  **Date**: 2026-03-28  **Language**: ja

> 一份详细的多分镜提示词，用于指导 Nano Banana Pro 生成灰度垂直四格浪漫喜剧漫画，讲述一名拥有时间停止能力的男子的故事，重点关注特定场景、角色表情以及日语对话。

![Nano Banana Pro 四格漫画提示词：时间停止喜剧](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774766206477_6q2b49_HEfaEDSbEAA21Md.jpg)

```
形式：縦4コマのグレースケール漫画
ジャンル：現代ラブコメ
絵柄：青年漫画、表情豊か
セリフ：吹き出しは日本語

1コマ目
シーン：
学生服の男の子が拳を握り、ドヤ顔でキラキラしたオーラを出している。
背景にキラキラ、効果線
吹き出しセリフ（日本語）：
「時間停止能力を手に入れたぞ！これで大好きなあの子と…！」

2コマ目
シーン：回想シーン、セリフなし、キラキラ演出

コマの中が3つくらいの小さな回想カットになっている。
・セーラー服の同級生の女の子に告白しているシーン（頬を赤らめている）
・大学時代、二人でデートしているシーン（私服で手をつないで笑顔）
・結婚式のシーン（ウェディングドレスとタキシード、横にペットの犬、祝福の紙吹雪）

全体がふわふわした光、ハートや花のトーン、キラキラ。
セリフなし。

3コマ目
シーン：新居のリビング、夜、落ち着いた雰囲気
大人になった男がソファに前のめりで座って真剣な顔、緊張した姿勢。顔の前で両手を組んだポーズ
生活感あるリビング（テーブル、カーテン、観葉植物など）。
吹き出しセリフ（日本語）：
「実は僕、時間停止能力があって、君と時間停止プレイしたいんだ」
男はめちゃくちゃ真剣

4コマ目
シーン：妻がツッコミ顔で立ち上がる
妻がびっくり顔で鋭いツッコミ、背景に衝撃の雷
後ろで犬が無邪気に「ハッハッ」と口を開けて笑顔、首をかしげて「？」マークが浮かんでいる。
吹き出しセリフ（日本語）：
「ここまで持ち込めたならもう必要なくない！？」
犬の横に小さく「？」。
```

**Author**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp)  **Date**: 2026-03-28  **Language**: ja

> 这是一份为 Nano Banana 2 编写的详细提示词，旨在生成一幅极繁主义杰作。该作品采用享誉全球的谷物艺术家周志江的风格，描绘了五种谷物，其排列方式参考了示例图像，背景为黄色小米，强调高分辨率与精细细节。

![适用于 Nano Banana 2 的极繁主义谷物艺术提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774766205832_1e2zsf_HEavoUVb0AA5kjn.jpg)

```
世界的に有名な穀物画の巨匠、周志江による、マキシマリスト様式の傑作。黄色い粟を背景に、5粒の穀物が参考画像のように配置されています。穀物本来の色合いと、その配置によって生み出される立体感が、絵画をより一層生き生きとさせています。高解像度、精緻な描写、超高精細、最高品質。
```

### 48. M DSLR 相机拆解与组装可视化

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-03-28  **Language**: en

> 为 Nano Banana 2 设计的两组不同图像提示词。第一组生成相机的拆解视图，第二组生成悬浮在空中并带有技术 UI 注释的高端相机产品可视化效果。第三组为 Kling AI 的动态提示词，此处已排除。

![M DSLR 相机拆解与组装可视化](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774766195170_7xt55w_HEe78o_aIAAEP89.jpg)

```
Image Prompt 1: Clearly separate all components with visible spacing. Move the lens forward and split it into several segments. Separate the camera body into three sections: upper section moves upward, left section moves left, right section moves right. Use elements present on the assembled camera, add electronic parts inside. No annotations.

Image Prompt 2: Create a realistic high-end product visualization of a fully assembled M DSLR camera with detachable lens floating slightly in the air. The device has a premium matte black body with subtle metallic details and engraved M branding. Background is a softly blurred modern tech environment with depth of field and subtle motion blur, no people visible. Cinematic studio lighting with realistic reflections and premium product rendering. Around the camera appear five minimalist technical UI annotations with thin lines pointing to components. Each annotation sits inside a small semi-transparent glass UI panel with soft glow and subtle cyan edge lighting, improving readability. Clean modern sans-serif typography.

Annotations:

24MP CMOS Sensor
4K Video Recording
Interchangeable Lens Mount
Fast Hybrid Autofocus
Optical Image Stabilization
```

```
舞台：ファンタジー世界、スラムの路地裏、薄暗い雰囲気、石畳と汚れた壁、ゴミや樽が置かれている

・粗野な男：冒険者崩れのアウトロー、顔に傷、無精ひげ、ボロい革装備、ガラが悪い醜男

真顔で女勇者の手はサムズアップ

【4コマ目】
```

```
{
  "vibe_title_en": "Tangible Melancholy",
  "master_prompt": "A hyper-realistic, close-up portrait of The Protagonist transformed into a living scrapbook, set within a sun-drenched, dusty antique restoration workshop. The subject's forehead and hair are adorned with physical, high-fidelity props: oversized glossy vintage campaign buttons, ceramic pins with hand-painted sad faces, and dried pressed wildflowers adhered to the skin with visible theatrical spirit gum. Words like 'fragile' and 'echo' are scrawled directly onto the cheekbones in smeared grease pencil, showcasing authentic skin texture and pores beneath the markings. The subject wears a delicate, antique lace collar that feels brittle to the touch. The lighting is soft, diffused northern window light, highlighting the dust motes dancing in the air and the microscopic scratches on the plastic buttons. Shot on a Hasselblad H6D-100c with an 80mm f/1.9 lens to create a razor-thin depth of field, blurring the background shelves filled with porcelain limbs and glass eyes. The color grade mimics Kodak Portra 160—soft, pastel, and slightly desaturated, emphasizing the tactile reality of this surreal emotional inventory.",
  "meta": {
    "intent": "Editorial Portraiture",
    "priorities": "Texture, Emotion, Surrealism",
    "device_profile": "High-End Medium Format"
  },
  "frame": {
    "aspect": "4:5",
    "composition": "Center-weighted close-up",
```

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-03-25  **Language**: en

> 一个针对 Nano Banana Pro 的技术提示，使用加权词 (::) 来生成一个 2D 示意图，该示意图由完全由印刷电路板 (PCB) 走线构成的“Tesla”字样组成。它指定了单色配色、技术矢量风格和平面照明，同时使用负面提示来排除逼真的纹理或颜色。

![PCB 文字艺术原理图： 'Tesla'](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774508262762_4ktyii_HEFZC2sXUAAg6AE.jpg)
![PCB 文字艺术原理图： 'Tesla'](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774508262843_2dluf1_HEFZC4NbAAAu4kU.jpg)

```
Anchor: The word "{argument name="word to construct" default="Tesla"}" :: constructed entirely from printed circuit board traces, where each letterform is a functional-looking PCB layout — solder pads as terminals, vias as joints, trace paths forming the strokes ::4 Morphology: Technical PCB illustration. Letter strokes are traces of varying widths. Circular vias punctuate stroke junctions. Solder pad rectangles anchor stroke terminals. The letters read as living circuit diagrams. Monochrome technical vector ::3 Material Physics: Jet black trace lines on white substrate, exposed copper-pad circles with concentric detail rings, uniform stroke weight with deliberate corner chamfers (45°) ::3 Illumination: Flat technical illustration lighting, no depth, pure 2D schematic clarity ::2 Render Stack: Electronics schematic aesthetic, hardware documentation style, Gerber file visual output ::1 Negative: [Silhouette shapes, actual electronic components, chip illustrations, realistic PCB green color, perspective, photographic textures, solder reflections] ::-1
```

### 150. 磨砂玻璃效果 提示词

**Author**: [Ege](https://x.com/egeberkina)  **Date**: 2026-03-24  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 Nano Banana 提示词，旨在将上传的图像转换，使其看起来像在厚重的磨砂玻璃面板后面，只有一个小的、清晰的窗口显示出锐利的细节。该提示词指定了视觉效果、构图和风格，以实现超现实的光学模拟。

![磨砂玻璃效果 提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421472597_k6d365_HEMR_DsW4AAKh4G.jpg)

```
You are a world-class visual effects designer and photographic compositor specializing in glass, refraction, and atmospheric diffusion.

Your task is to transform the uploaded image so that it appears behind a thick foggy frosted glass panel, while keeping only a very small selected region crystal clear.

INPUT IMAGE:
[UPLOAD IMAGE]

INSTRUCTIONS:

• Cover the entire image with a realistic frosted glass / fogged glass texture
• The glass should create heavy diffusion, grainy micro-distortion, and refractive blur
• The effect should resemble bathroom privacy glass or heavily steamed window glass

• The distortion must include:

micro ripples
refractive glass warping
light scattering
blurred shapes behind the glass

• Only a very small area must remain perfectly clear

a narrow horizontal opening or small window
sharp, fully visible detail inside that region
the rest of the image remains strongly diffused

• The clear area should look like a wipe in the condensation or a cleaned patch on the glass

GLASS EFFECT DETAILS:

• high density frosted glass texture
• strong diffusion and noise pattern
• subtle depth refraction
• irregular organic blur pattern
• soft lighting scattering through the glass

STYLE:

• hyper realistic optical glass simulation
• photographic quality
• cinematic lighting
• modern editorial design aesthetic

COMPOSITION:

• subject visible through glass
• tiny clear window revealing key detail (eyes / face / object)
• rest of the frame heavily frosted and distorted

IMPORTANT:

The frosted glass must look physically real, not a simple blur filter.
The clear region must be sharp and untouched, creating strong contrast with the fogged glass surface.
```

[[Image Transformation]] [[Optical Illusion]]

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2026-03-24  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张未来主义的、电影般的图像：哈利法塔的建筑蓝图以发光、动态构建的全息图形式，投射在一张高科技玻璃桌上方。该提示详细说明了从线框图到照片级真实结构的过渡，以及灯光（霓虹蓝/青色）和环境（极简主义建筑实验室）的设定。

![未来感全息迪拜哈利法塔蓝图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421477128_lcgq2f_HEMIVaQa0AAqry1.jpg)
![未来感全息迪拜哈利法塔蓝图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421477343_u93biq_HEMIVZgbEAAdKD0.jpg)

```
CONCEPT:
A futuristic architectural blueprint of the Burj Khalifa projected as a glowing hologram, actively constructing itself in mid-air through robotic precision and digital intelligence.

SUBJECT:
A semi-transparent holographic version of the Burj Khalifa floating above a sleek glass smart table. The lower portion appears as a glowing blue wireframe blueprint, while the upper portion transitions into a fully photorealistic skyscraper with reflective glass panels and metallic structure as it builds itself in real-time.

ENVIRONMENT:
A high-tech architectural lab with a dark, minimal interior. The blueprint originates from a glossy black glass table embedded with touch controls, glowing UI panels, and soft neon edges. Subtle reflections of the hologram appear on the table surface. Background is clean, futuristic, and slightly blurred.

STRUCTURAL DETAILS:
The central spire rises as glowing gridlines before solidifying into steel and glass  
Tiered setbacks of the tower assemble through hovering robotic drones  
Glass facade panels lock into place with precise alignment and reflections  
Laser beams scan and map each level during construction  
Small AI drones orbit around the structure, actively building and welding components  
Materials transition from holographic light into real textures — polished glass, steel beams, and concrete core  
Floating UI overlays show measurements, grids, and rotating architectural schematics

VISUAL MECHANIC:
The blueprint exists in layered form — base is a glowing grid, mid-layer is a semi-transparent wireframe, and top layer is fully realistic. Certain sections flicker between hologram and solid material, emphasizing the transformation.

LIGHTING:
Dark environment with strong neon blue and cyan holographic glow. Subtle rim lighting created by reflections from the hologram. Volumetric light beams and soft particles enhance depth.

CAMERA & LENS:
Shot on a full-frame camera, 35mm lens. Slight low-angle perspective to emphasize scale and height. Sharp focus on the hologram core with slight background blur.

COMPOSITION:
Vertical 2:3 format. The Burj Khalifa hologram is centered, rising upward. UI elements orbit symmetrically around it. Clean negative space enhances the futuristic aesthetic.

STYLE & MOOD:
Futuristic, cinematic, high-tech, and minimal. Feels like advanced AI-driven architecture and innovation. Clean, premium, and visually striking.

DETAILS:
Ultra-sharp holographic lines, glowing particles, realistic glass reflections, smooth transitions between digital and physical materials, micro UI details, 8K resolution, HDR, cinematic color grading with blue/cyan tones and deep contrast.

NEGATIVE PROMPT:
cluttered environment, low detail, dull lighting, messy UI, cartoon style, distorted structure, blurry hologram, watermark
```

### 153. Bat Cowl Protocol 角色提示

**Author**: [Edizkan ⭕🦇](https://x.com/edizkan_)  **Date**: 2026-03-24  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的提示，用于让 Nano Banana（或 Gemini Nano Banana）生成一个高质量的 设计师玩具角色 3D 渲染图，同时将 参考图片 中的一个定制 'Bat Cowl' 整合到该角色上，并严格保持该角色原有的服装、形象和光照条件。

![Bat Cowl Protocol 角色提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421473775_ksdvy8_HELkjkWaIAEqNjn.jpg)

```
A high-quality 3D render of the designer toy from [Reference Image 1]. Requirement: The character must retain its exact original outfit . The Mask: Tightly fit a custom "Bat Cowl" ([Reference Image 2]) over the head.

The Cowl: Must match the exact color, material, and design, with size adjusted as needed to fit the reference character’s head.
Scaling: Tailored, bespoke fit with a shortened chin guard precisely following the character's jawline. Cowl size is adjusted to match the reference character exactly. The cowl fits seamlessly, with no gap between the head and the chin guard.
Ears: Only the sharp bat ears are visible; hide original ears, headwears, horn, accessories, hat, helmet entirely.
The Cutout: The cowl features a cutout area; through this opening, the underlying part of the reference character must be visible exactly as it is, with no additions, removals, or alterations.
Eyes: Use the exact glowing eye effect from the reference cowl image.
Constraint: No nose or eyes should be rendered on the cowl or the character's face.
8k, studio lighting, Background must match the reference character’s background exactly.
Lighting
Lighting should match the reference character’s original light behavior, and the cowl must follow and respond to the same lighting conditions.
Character Likeness Integrity (CRITICAL)

Maintain the exact eye shape, spacing, stylization, patterns, silhouette, and original color palette from the reference.

Do not humanize.

Do not alter anatomy.

Do not modify facial structure.

Identity must remain instantly recognizable.

If the character wears a balaclava, mask, helmet, or covered face, don't invent facial anatomy.
No added nose.

No added mouth.

No visible skin where the reference does not show it.
```

### 157. 霍格沃茨 大礼堂 在 雷暴 中

**Author**: [Akshen](https://x.com/akshen121)  **Date**: 2026-03-24  **Language**: en

> 一个描述性提示词，用于生成霍格沃茨大礼堂在雷暴中的戏剧性场景。该提示词具体描述了施了魔法的天花板上闪现着狂暴的闪电，数千支摇曳的漂浮蜡烛，以及雨水在学生们头顶上方蒸发，强调了哥特式建筑和迷蒙的黑暗。此提示词适用于 Nano Banana Pro、Midjourney v8 和 Uni -1。

![霍格沃茨 大礼堂 在 雷暴 中](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421483152_kkkv13_HEK0-eeaIAEbCKy.jpg)

### 169. Nano Banana 2 Brushstroke Title Logo 提示词（4 种风格）

**Author**: [なお](https://x.com/Naonekozamurai)  **Date**: 2026-03-23  **Language**: ja

> 使用 Nano Banana 2 生成四种不同风格笔触标题 Logo 的详细提示词，涵盖热血动漫（Battle Anime）、缤纷流行（Colorful Pop）、恐怖（Horror）及赛博朋克（Cyberpunk）风格。用户只需将占位符 {TEXT} 替换为所需的标题即可。

![Nano Banana 2 Brushstroke Title Logo 提示词（4 种风格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334476231_0emrm3_HEIE7_IaIAICL_T.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 Brushstroke Title Logo 提示词（4 种风格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334476167_tco6jh_HEIE9rKaUAASqY-.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 Brushstroke Title Logo 提示词（4 种风格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334476259_hlu641_HEIE-8ibcAAkz1Y.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 Brushstroke Title Logo 提示词（4 种风格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334477003_kvkvud_HEIFAEqaIAAoKBA.jpg)

```
1、バトルアニメ系：
「テキスト「{argument name="テキスト" default="TEXT"}」のタイトルロゴ。
荒々しく勢いのある筆文字、墨の飛沫とにじみ、激しいブラシストローク。
背景に爆発的なエネルギー、炎、雷、スピードライン。
少年漫画のバトル作品のタイトルのような迫力。
ハイコントラスト、発光エフェクト、ドラマチック、ダイナミック構図、4K。
背景画像や風景、装飾的なシーンは一切含めない。
背景は完全な単色（白または黒）または透明。」

2、カラフルポップ系：
「テキスト「{argument name="テキスト" default="TEXT"}」のタイトルロゴ。
筆文字フォントだがポップでカラフル、墨にネオンカラーやグラデーションを融合。
インクスプラッシュとポップな図形（円や星）を組み合わせる。
アニメOPのロゴのような明るく印象的なデザイン。
鮮やかな色彩、クリーンで高解像度。
背景画像や風景、装飾的なシーンは一切含めない。
背景は完全な単色（白または黒）または透明。」

3、ホラー系：
「テキスト「{argument name="テキスト" default="TEXT"}」のタイトルロゴ。

歪みや揺らぎのある不気味な筆文字、崩れかけた書道、細く伸びる異様なストローク。
墨は黒だけでなく、血のようににじむ赤黒いインク、滴るような表現、粘度のある質感。
かすれやにじみが強く、不規則で不安定な形状。

文字の一部が溶ける、滲む、崩れるような異常表現。
わずかにブレや二重像（ゴースト）を含む。

エフェクト：
・弱く不気味に発光する縁取り（赤または青白い光）
・霧のような薄いスモーク
・ノイズ、グリッチ、粒子のざらつき
・血の飛沫のようなインクスプラッシュ（控えめ）

全体として静かな恐怖、不安感、違和感を強調。
ジャパニーズホラーやサイコホラー映画のタイトルのような雰囲気。

高コントラスト、ダークトーン、シネマティック、超高精細、4K、masterpiece、best quality、ultra detailed、typography、logo design
背景画像や風景、装飾的なシーンは一切含めない。
背景は完全な単色（白または黒）または透明。」

4、サイバーパンク系：
「テキスト「{argument name="テキスト" default="TEXT"}」のタイトルロゴ。

未来的で洗練されたサイバーパンクスタイルのデザイン。
筆文字をベースにしつつ、ストロークの一部がデジタル的に変形・再構築されたハイブリッド書体。

滑らかでシャープな線と、幾何学的でテクノロジー感のあるエッジを融合。
墨の表現はクリーンで、にじみは最小限またはスタイライズされた形に変換。

カラーはネオン（シアン、マゼンタ、パープル、ブルー）を基調に、
発光するラインや縁取り、グラデーションで構成。

エフェクト：
・グリッチ（軽めでスタイリッシュ）
・ホログラム風の透明感
・光の粒子やデジタルノイズ
・走査線、UI風の細かいラインや断片

文字の一部がピクセル化、分解、再構築される未来的演出。

クリーン、シャープ、ハイコントラスト、発光、未来的、
超高精細、4K、masterpiece、best quality、ultra detailed、typography、logo design
背景画像や風景、装飾的なシーンは一切含めない。
背景は完全な単色（白または黒）または透明。」
```

[[Logo Design]]

### 170. 针对 Nano Banana Pro 的 9 宫格编辑风格提示词

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-03-23  **Language**: en

> 针对 Nano Banana Pro 的一份高度详细且结构化的提示词，旨在生成一张写实风格的 3x3 杂志编辑网格图。图中包含同一位优雅女性的九种不同且充满力量感的舞蹈姿势，并保持其身份特征、发型、妆容及着装的高度一致，背景则设定为充满氛围感的奢华摄影棚。

![针对 Nano Banana Pro 的 9 宫格编辑风格提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334458195_chgsac_HEHzSFaaIAEMFIh.jpg)

```
Create a photoreal 3x3 editorial grid featuring the same elegant adult woman in all nine panels. Keep the same woman and the same facial identity across every panel, but update the styling to feel more striking, glamorous, and visually powerful. Use the same hair and same makeup in all nine panels for consistency, but change the outfit and background from the previous concept. The woman should wear one dramatic fashion-dance look in all panels: a sleek dark burgundy or black-wine fitted performance set with a sculptural asymmetric top, subtle sheen, refined cutouts or draped details, and matching fitted bottoms or a fashion-dance silhouette that feels expensive and cinematic. The background should be the same in all panels: a moody luxury editorial studio with a deep burgundy-to-black gradient, glossy shadow depth, and premium cinematic atmosphere. Only the pose and subtle expression should change from panel to panel. Every pose must feel more impactful, stronger, more elegant, and more unforgettable than ordinary dance poses. Use long extended body lines, deep curves through the torso, dramatic arm architecture, controlled turns, seated power poses, off-balance fashion shapes, stretched leg lines, and expressive stage presence. The result should feel like one cohesive luxury dance campaign with nine powerful moments from the same shoot. Subject: one woman with identical facial features across all nine panels, same soft glamorous dark hair with elegant movement in all panels, same dark burgundy or black-wine fashion dance outfit in all panels (sculptural, fitted, refined, cinematic, luxurious), same polished editorial makeup in all panels (luminous skin, defined eyes, rich elegant finish). Scene: same moody luxury studio with a deep burgundy-to-black gradient background in all panels, dramatic, sensual, refined, powerful, cinematic, fashion-forward mood. Panel directions: Panel 1: strong standing pose with one arm arched overhead and the other extended low, long diagonal body line. Panel 2: twisted torso pose with a deep shoulder turn and elegant intense gaze, subtle movement in the hair. Panel 3: high-impact side pose with one leg lengthened and both arms forming a sculptural frame. Panel 4: dynamic leaning pose with dramatic spine curve and expressive hand placement. Panel 5: center hero pose, grounded and commanding, with poised torso and unforgettable editorial energy. Panel 6: one-leg lifted pose with strong balance, stretched foot line, and bold arm extension. Panel 7: low seated or floor-based pose with luxurious body curve and powerful fashion attitude. Panel 8: overhead crossed-arm pose with elongated torso and elegant tension through the neck and shoulders. Panel 9: final campaign-finishing pose with a deep side extension, refined hand line, and strong cinematic silhouette. Camera: mixed medium, three-quarter, full-body, and floor-based fashion portrait compositions, cinematic editorial studio angles, focus sharp on face, outfit texture, silhouette, and dance body lines, clean premium studio separation depth of field. Lighting: controlled cinematic studio lighting, soft sculpting with deeper contrast, elegant highlights, and premium shadow shaping, realistic skin texture, no plastic effect. Must have: 3x3 grid layout, same woman in all panels, same hair in all panels, same makeup in all panels, same new outfit in all panels, same new background in all panels, different pose in every panel, more impactful dance-fashion poses, photoreal quality, perfect anatomy, realistic hands, physically accurate posture and balance, sharp face in every panel, no text anywhere. Negative prompt: different identity in each panel, different outfit in each panel, different hair in each panel, different background in each panel, weak posing, static posing, awkward limbs, bad anatomy, extra fingers, missing fingers, deformed hands, broken wrists, stiff shoulders, unnatural spine, plastic skin, blurry face, duplicate limbs, cartoon, low detail, text, logo, watermark. Output settings: 4:5 portrait aspect ratio, ultra high resolution, 1 image, 3x3 grid with thin gutter, no outer border, maximum panel consistency, cinematic luxury editorial realism style, editorial crisp sharpness, subtle film grain, rich high end dynamic range, burgundy noir editorial color grade.
```

### 174. Nano Banana 2 的物体推理测试提示词

**Author**: [Harshith](https://x.com/HarshithLucky3)  **Date**: 2026-03-23  **Language**: en

> 一段详细的提示词，旨在测试图像生成模型（对比 Nano Banana 2 和 Uni-1）的物体推理与空间感知能力。该提示词要求对特定物体（红色立方体、黄色球体、绿色马克杯、银色烛台）进行精准布局，并设定了一个复杂的反射场景——即绿色马克杯不会出现在镜子中。

![Nano Banana 2 的物体推理测试提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334459639_j9sygd_HEHGxg8aIAUSTJf.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 的物体推理测试提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334459801_swdutp_HEHGybXaIAAjK_D.jpg)

```
A photorealistic studio shot. On a wooden table sits a solid red cube. Resting exactly on top of the red cube is a glowing yellow sphere. Directly to the left of the red cube is a green ceramic coffee mug. Directly behind the red cube is a tall, ornate silver candlestick. Behind all of these objects is a large, clear mirror reflecting the scene. In the mirror's reflection, the red cube, the yellow sphere, and the silver candlestick are perfectly reflected, but the green ceramic coffee mug is completely absent from the reflection. The space where the green mug should be in the mirror shows only the empty wooden table.
```

### 180. Nano Banana 2 角色协作菜单 Prompt

**Author**: [絵空事テレビ / AIカワウソ](https://x.com/boke_ai)  **Date**: 2026-03-23  **Language**: ja

> 一个针对 Nano Banana 2 的详细提示词模板，用于根据提供的角色图像和设定，生成一份家庭餐厅联名菜单的图像。该提示词明确了输出格式、风格以及内容细节。

![Nano Banana 2 角色协作菜单 Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334473395_7zuq71_HEFSSXEaQAAq8T8.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 角色协作菜单 Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334473644_cvpl6k_HEFSY_9awAAJ7rQ.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 角色协作菜单 Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334474010_3nxxcw_HEFSWdjacAEpMwd.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 角色协作菜单 Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774334474653_8s9vl3_HEFSZ5TbAAAYScp.jpg)

```
【キャラ設定】
- キャラ名：[{argument name="キャラクター名" default=""}]　← ここだけ埋めればOK。以下は任意
- 色・見た目の特徴：[{argument name="色・見た目の特徴" default=""}]
- 性格・口癖・行動パターン：[{argument name="性格・口癖・行動パターン" default=""}]
- 世界観・所属・設定：[{argument name="世界観・所属・設定" default=""}]
- ネタ・笑いのポイント：[{argument name="ネタ・笑いのポイント" default=""}]
※空欄の項目はすべて添付画像から読み取って自由に補完してください。キャラ名も空欄の場合は画像から命名してください。

上記のキャラクター設定と添付画像を使った「[{argument name="キャラクター名" default=""}]フェア」のファミリーレストランコラボメニューを作成。

出力形式：
実際のファミレスのテーブルの上に置かれた光沢のある冊子メニューを斜め上から撮影した写真風画像。冊子は見開きで開いており、ページには実際の料理写真・価格・メニュー番号が印刷されている。テーブルの木目や冊子の影・反射など、リアルな撮影環境の質感を再現すること。

メニューの内容：
- ページ上部に「[{argument name="キャラクター名" default=""}]フェア」のロゴ（食欲をそそるポップな赤×黄×白の配色）
- メニューページ内のキャラクター表現は添付画像のスタイルに合わせること：添付がイラスト・アニメ調ならイラストで、実写・写真調なら実写人物の写真で再現する。いずれも添付のビジュアルを忠実に反映すること。ポーズは以下からランダムに1つ選ぶ：①トレーを両手で差し出す ②料理を指差してアピール ③エプロン姿でガッツポーズ ④走りながら料理を運ぶ ⑤テーブルに身を乗り出しておすすめを囁く
- 上記キャラ設定をもとにオリジナルメニュー3品を考案。キャラの見た目・口癖・ネタを料理名や説明文に直接反映させること。各品に料理名・説明文・価格（税込）・メニュー番号を記載
- 「期間限定」「数量限定」のバナーをページ内に配置

横長の見開き構成（左ページにキャラ×メニュー紹介、右ページに料理写真×価格一覧）。
```

[[Graphic Design]]

### 182. 巴黎高级时装编辑三联画提示，适用于 Nano Banana Pro

**Author**: [Minahil](https://x.com/Minahil42298354)  **Date**: 2026-03-23  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Gemini Nano Banana (Nano Banana Pro) 设计的详细图像生成提示，要求创作一幅以巴黎女性为主题的高级时装编辑三联画，重点突出一条从她连衣裙上散开的红色线头沿着鹅卵石街道蜿蜒的超现实细节。

![巴黎高级时装编辑三联画提示，适用于 Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774248327496_oc96jd_HEE168fbUAACcRp.jpg)

```
A high-fashion editorial triptych featuring a young French woman with a messy brunette bob and a natural smile. She is wearing a long, form-fitting knit dress with horizontal red and white stripes, paired with classic brown leather loafers and a vintage crossbody bag. The style is effortlessly elegant with a "je ne sais quoi" Parisian vibe.
​The Surreal Detail:
The focal point is the hem of the dress, which is visibly unraveled. A single, vibrant red thread of yarn has come loose and extends outward, trailing behind her along the cobblestone street like a thin, continuous line, connecting her to an unseen point in the distance.
​Setting & Atmosphere:
​Location: A narrow, historic street in Paris with beige stone buildings and a traditional "TABAC" brasserie in the background.
​Lighting: Soft, overcast daylight that brings out the richness of the red yarn and the texture of the cobblestones.
​Composition: A three-panel layout showing a close-up of the frayed hem, a full-length shot of her walking, and a medium shot focusing on her expression and the dress texture.
```

[[Cobblestone Street]]

### 191. 3x3 极简舞蹈编辑网格

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-03-22  **Language**: en

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 生成 3x3 超逼真极简舞蹈时尚编辑网格的结构化提示。图像中有一位始终如一的女性模特，留着黑色短波波头，身穿白色露脐上衣和超大黑色裤子，在干净的白色工作室环境中表演九种不同的富有表现力、流畅的舞蹈姿势。
